# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
What makes a fraction "improper"? 
If the degree of numerator is greater than or equal to the degree of the denominator ^1FInGVXb

Questions might take one of two forms:
- Do the division to express as a quotient and a remainder

- Express as partial fractions ^DNEoS90s

Degree of numerator - degree of denominator = degree of quotient ^QQdA7Rd0
